# Top 50 Reaction Time Reduction Exercise Cards

## Source and caveat

exercise_card_details_for_llm.md was used as the governing Card v2 authoring source for phase-first card creation, canonical phase keys, subrole/slot logic, taxonomy key+weight tags, movement requirements, coaching execution, dosage, scaling cohorts, safety, regimen, phaseProfile, publish gates, and common anti-patterns. Purpose.txt was requested, but no literal Purpose.txt file was located in the accessible File Library search results for this run; this caveat is preserved instead of pretending it was read. Exercise selection is therefore grounded in the Card v2 guide, existing Vortex perception-action and neural-output card patterns surfaced in the File Library, the user-stated focus (reaction time reduction), and stable coaching expertise.

## Authoring rule

Use camelCase Card v2 Authoring JSON: identity fields, canonical primaryPhaseKey, subrole, slot, taxonomy arrays using key+weight, movementRequirements, coachingExecution, dosage, scaling cohorts, pairing logic, safety, regimen, and phaseProfile. Reaction-time work is quality-first: short exposures, clear stimulus, adequate rest, and immediate stop when decision quality, posture, braking, spacing, or reset behavior degrades.

## Category map

- **01-10 — Simple Cue Response & Start Reaction**: Low-fatigue visual, auditory, and tactile cue drills that reduce start latency and teach athletes to wait for the signal before moving cleanly.
- **11-20 — Visual Tracking, Catch, and Hand-Eye Reaction**: Object-tracking drills that connect eyes, hands, feet, and trunk organization so the athlete can identify the cue and answer accurately.
- **21-30 — Mirror, Partner, and Opponent Read**: Partner-generated live cues that train body-language reading, first-step timing, spacing, braking, and safe reset behavior.
- **31-40 — Reactive Change of Direction, Braking, and Re-Acceleration**: Short COD tasks that link cue recognition to cut angle, braking timing, foot placement, re-acceleration, and clean deceleration.
- **41-50 — Spatial Awareness, Multi-Cue, and Game Constraint Reaction**: Spatially rich drills that require scanning, reorientation, collision avoidance, boundary awareness, and controlled multi-cue decisions.
